<user_name>Nathan Delaney</user_name>< Text>
Finally got around to trying out.  I tried coming here for lunch a few months ago, but had no luck finding any people to order from.  This last time was better, we grabbed our own menus and withing a couple minutes we were acknowledged.  Service here seems to be the main issue.  When we were seated we were one of 3 tables and as lunch went on it got up to about 8.  It took awhile to get waters, table settings, our beverages, and refills were very few.  Our request for extra napkins didn't come until near the end of the meal.  The check suffered the same issue.  Instead of working multiple tables at once with simple things like napkins, water, and checks the service was one table at a time.  Extremely inefficient and was really strange to see.

That being said, the food made the strange service issues worth it.  I had been here for Thai food before and the food was good.  But, I've been into the cuban food lately as more and more trickles into the west coast.  I'd heard mixed things about the cubano, but the last I had seen looked very promising.  I ordered the Tampa cubano since they say Tampa invented it supposedly.  The sandwich came out hot and freshly pressed.  It was larger than I had anticipated, otherwise probably would have split it.  The side of the plantain chips is a really nice touch.  The pulled pork, ham, salami, cheese, pickles and mustard are blended so well!  Definitely the best cubano I have had thus far in California.  The pickles were nice and thick and the mustard was plentiful.  The pork was tender and lightly seasoned and the ham and salami are as to be expected from a processed meat.  I will definitely be calling in orders of the sandwiches in the future, this was killer.  What a great hidden gem in Morro Bay with great Cuban food, I can't wait to taste the rest of the menu.<//Text>

Service was good and pleasant enough. The food on the other hand was less than unimpressive. The food (pad thai and I think a curry dish) was bland. I suspect it was reheated. We heard the microwave beep several times while we waited for our food. We were the only two in the restaurant at the time so I doubt there would be anyone else to reheat anything for.  When we got the dishes they were unevenly heated and gave both my girlfriend and I the impression that our dishes were probably reheated from frozen. Not terrible and didn't make me sick but the taste of the meat was off and the sauce surrounding everything was extremely oily. We were starving and it thoroughly quashed our appetites for all the wrong reasons. Left more than half of our plates uneaten.

To the owner: I apologize for the bad review but it's the truth. I would suggest pairing down the menu to only serve dishes that you can cook fresh on the spot amd maybe use a little less sauce.<//Text>

Very long wait, inadequate service:
We went to Thai Bounty last night, we were there before 6:00 p.m. and didn't leave until 8:00. We were a party of seven, however when we arrived at the restaurant there were few customers. Our appetizers came quickly, however after that it took about an hour to receive our food. Everyone in our party was upset, especially when noticing that people who arrived after us had received their meals, and even left the restaurant.  The servers did not acknowledge the wait time until our food was almost ready, and one dish was still not prepared and was received about 10 minutes after everyone else. The staff was not apologetic, and all 7 of us were not happy with the experience. We have always supported the Thai restaurants of the mutual families who own several restaurants in the area, but Thai Bounty won't be one of them. The only reason I did not give a lower rating is overall The food was good, except two people who ordered the Bay scallops did not enjoy their meals, one couldn't eat hers.< /Text>

I have been a customer at this location for several years.  The facility is well maintained and secure.   There is a restroom available at the office building which is maintained well  and can be used as long as the facility is open  (even after office hours).
